    def _attach_video_render_manifest(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        artifacts = self._collect_video_artifacts(task=task, result=normalized_result)
        if not artifacts:
            return normalized_result

        render_manifest = self._build_video_render_manifest(
            task=task,
            result=normalized_result,
            artifacts=artifacts,
        )
        normalized_result["artifacts"] = artifacts
        normalized_result["render_manifest"] = render_manifest
        return normalized_result

    def _collect_video_artifacts(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
        output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        named_output_path = str(result.get("named_output_path") or "").strip()
        original_output_path = str(result.get("original_output_path") or "").strip()
        preferred_primary_path = output_path or named_output_path or original_output_path
        primary_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(preferred_primary_path)

        candidate_files: Dict[str, Path] = {}
        for raw_path in (output_path, named_output_path, original_output_path):
            resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(raw_path)
            if resolved is not None:
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        candidate_dirs: List[Path] = []
        for raw_dir in (
            str(task_dir),
            str(Path(output_path).parent) if output_path else "",
            str(Path(named_output_path).parent) if named_output_path else "",
            str(Path(original_output_path).parent) if original_output_path else "",
        ):
            resolved_dir = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(raw_dir)
            if resolved_dir is None:
                continue
            if resolved_dir not in candidate_dirs:
                candidate_dirs.append(resolved_dir)

        for base_dir in candidate_dirs:
            try:
                files = sorted(
                    [path for path in base_dir.rglob("*") if path.is_file()],
                    key=lambda item: str(item).lower(),
                )
            except Exception:
                continue
            for path in files:
                if not self._should_expose_video_artifact(path):
                    continue
                resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(str(path))
                if resolved is None:
                    continue
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        used_ids: set[str] = set()
        task_dir_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(str(task_dir))
        sorted_files = sorted(
            candidate_files.values(),
            key=lambda item: self._video_artifact_sort_key(
                path=item,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            ),
        )
        single_artifact_roles = {
            "final_video",
            "video_subtitled",
            "video_no_subtitle",
            "coverless_video",
            "subtitle_srt",
            "subtitle_ass",
            "transcript_text",
            "clip_text",
            "forum_post_info",
            "cover_image",
            "cover_manifest",
            "processing_log",
            "pipeline_state",
            "video",
        }
        selected_files: List[Tuple[Path, str, str]] = []
        seen_roles: set[str] = set()
        for path in sorted_files:
            role, kind = self._classify_video_artifact_role(
                path=path,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            )
            if role in single_artifact_roles and role in seen_roles:
                continue
            seen_roles.add(role)
            selected_files.append((path, role, kind))

        for index, artifact_info in enumerate(selected_files, start=1):
            path, role, kind = artifact_info
            artifact_id = self._build_video_artifact_id(
                role=role,
                index=index,
                used_ids=used_ids,
            )
            relative_path = self._build_artifact_relative_path(path=path, task_dir=task_dir_resolved)
            stat = path.stat()
            artifacts.append(
                {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "kind": kind,
                    "role": role,
                    "filename": path.name,
                    "path": str(path),
                    "relative_path": relative_path,
                    "size_bytes": int(stat.st_size),
                    "is_primary": primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved,
                }
            )
        return artifacts

    def _build_video_render_manifest(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        result: Dict[str, Any],
        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        primary_artifact_id = ""
        videos: Dict[str, str] = {}
        subtitles: Dict[str, str] = {}
        texts: Dict[str, str] = {}
        context: Dict[str, str] = {}
        logs: Dict[str, str] = {}
        cover: Dict[str, str] = {}
        pipeline_state: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        for artifact in artifacts:
            artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
            role = str(artifact.get("role") or "").strip()
            path_text = str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip()
            if artifact.get("is_primary") and artifact_id:
                primary_artifact_id = artifact_id

            if role == "final_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["primary"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_subtitled" and artifact_id and "subtitled" not in videos:
                videos["subtitled"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_no_subtitle" and artifact_id:
                videos["no_subtitle"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "coverless_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["coverless"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video" and artifact_id and "alternate" not in videos:
                videos["alternate"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_srt" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["srt"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_ass" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["ass"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "transcript_text" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["script"] = artifact_id
                texts["script"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "clip_text" and artifact_id:
                texts["clip_text"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "forum_post_info" and artifact_id:
                context["forum_post_info"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_image" and artifact_id and "image" not in cover:
                cover["image"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_manifest" and artifact_id:
                cover["manifest"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "processing_log" and artifact_id and "processing" not in logs:
                logs["processing"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "pipeline_state" and artifact_id:
                pipeline_state = {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "path": path_text,
                }
                pipeline_state.update(self._read_pipeline_state_summary(path_text))

        manifest: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "task_id": task.task_id,
            "artifact_count": len(artifacts),
            "primary_artifact_id": primary_artifact_id,
            "primary_output_path": str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
            "videos": videos,
            "subtitles": subtitles,
            "cover": cover,
        }
        if texts:
            manifest["texts"] = texts
        if context:
            manifest["context"] = context
        if logs:
            manifest["logs"] = logs
        if pipeline_state:
            manifest["pipeline_state"] = pipeline_state
        return manifest

    def _safe_resolve_existing_path(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_file():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _safe_resolve_existing_dir(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_dir():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _should_expose_video_artifact(self, path: Path) -> bool:
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        name = path.name.lower()
        video_exts = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
        image_exts = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}
        if suffix in video_exts or suffix in image_exts:
            return True
        if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass", "script.txt", "state.json"}:
            return True
        if name in {"clip_text.txt", "forum_post_info.json"}:
            return True
        if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in name:
            return True
        if suffix == ".log":
            return True
        return False

    def _classify_video_artifact_role(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
        text = path.name.lower()
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        if primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved:
            return "final_video", "video"

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Iterable

from apps.api.openclaw_client import run_openclaw_video_task


def _parse_args(argv: Iterable[str] | None = None) -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Submit CloneCut video task and fetch OpenClaw-friendly result")
    parser.add_argument("--api-base", default="http://127.0.0.1:18100", help="CloneCut API base URL")
    parser.add_argument("--file", required=True, help="Local video path to upload")
    parser.add_argument("--api-token", default="", help="CloneCut API token, optional")
    parser.add_argument("--api-token-env", default="CLONECUT_API_TOKEN", help="fallback env name for api token")
    parser.add_argument("--task-id", default="", help="optional explicit task id")
    parser.add_argument("--source", default="openclaw_client", help="task source marker")
    parser.add_argument("--stage5-model-name", default="", help="stage5 model name or backend model id")
    parser.add_argument("--clip-text", default="", help="optional explicit clip text override")
    parser.add_argument("--post-url", default="", help="optional forum post url")
    parser.add_argument("--no-wait", action="store_true", help="only submit task without polling result")
    parser.add_argument("--submit-timeout-seconds", type=float, default=30.0, help="submit request timeout")
    parser.add_argument("--wait-timeout-seconds", type=float, default=1800.0, help="poll total timeout")
    parser.add_argument("--poll-interval-seconds", type=float, default=5.0, help="poll interval")
    parser.add_argument("--request-timeout-seconds", type=float, default=15.0, help="single polling request timeout")
    parser.add_argument("--output-json", default="", help="optional path to persist final json result")
    return parser.parse_args(list(argv) if argv is not None else None)


def main(argv: Iterable[str] | None = None) -> int:
    args = _parse_args(argv)
    api_token = str(args.api_token or "").strip() or str(os.getenv(args.api_token_env, "") or "").strip()

    extra_form: dict[str, str] = {}
    if args.clip_text:
        extra_form["clip_text"] = str(args.clip_text)
    if args.post_url:
        extra_form["post_url"] = str(args.post_url)

    payload = run_openclaw_video_task(
        api_base=args.api_base,
        video_path=args.file,
        api_token=api_token,
        task_id=args.task_id,
        source=args.source,
        stage5_model_name=args.stage5_model_name,
        extra_form=extra_form,
        wait=not bool(args.no_wait),
        submit_timeout_seconds=float(args.submit_timeout_seconds),
        wait_timeout_seconds=float(args.wait_timeout_seconds),
        poll_interval_seconds=float(args.poll_interval_seconds),
        request_timeout_seconds=float(args.request_timeout_seconds),
    )
    text = json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    print(text)

    output_json = str(args.output_json or "").strip()
    if output_json:
        output_path = Path(output_json).expanduser()
        output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        output_path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")
    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

    def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
        state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
        if not state_file.exists():
            raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
        try:
            payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception as exc:
            raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc

        last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
        if last_completed_step < 9:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
            )
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            candidate = Path(output_file)
            if candidate.exists():
                return candidate

        patterns = [
            f"{source_path.stem}*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
            "*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
            "*.mp4",
        ]
        for pattern in patterns:
            candidates = [
                p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
                if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
            ]
            if candidates:
                candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
                return candidates[0]

        raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")

        self,

        source: Path,
        task_dir: Path,

    def _run_process_stage(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PROCESSING)
        task.stage_checkpoint = "process"
        self._persist_task(task)
        self.logger.info("task processing started: task_id=%s", task.task_id)

        try:
            if task.task_type in {TaskType.TTS, TaskType.VOICE_CLONE}:
                result = self._process_tts_like(task)
            else:
                result = self._process_video_like(task)
            if task.task_type == TaskType.VIDEO:
                result = self._apply_video_output_naming(task, result)
                result = self._attach_video_render_manifest(task, result)

            task.result = result
            task.output_path = result.get("output_path")
            if task.output_path and task.output_path not in task.output_files:
                task.output_files.append(task.output_path)
            task.error_message = None
            self._persist_task(task)

            if task.output_path and Path(task.output_path).exists():
                self._enqueue_task("upload", task)
                return
            self._complete_task(task)
        except Exception as exc:
            self._fail_task(task, exc, failed_from=TaskStatus.PROCESSING)

    def _run_upload_stage(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.UPLOADING)
        task.stage_checkpoint = "upload"
        self._persist_task(task)
        self.logger.info("task uploading started: task_id=%s", task.task_id)
        started = time.perf_counter()

        try:
            upload_result = self._upload_output(task)
            upload_result["duration_ms"] = int(max(0.0, (time.perf_counter() - started) * 1000))
            result = dict(task.result or {})
            result["upload"] = upload_result
            task.result = result
            task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
            task.metadata["upload_duration_ms"] = upload_result["duration_ms"]
            task.error_message = None
            self._persist_task(task)
            self._complete_task(task)
        except Exception as exc:
            self._fail_task(task, exc, failed_from=TaskStatus.UPLOADING)

    def _dequeue_stage_task(self, stage: str) -> Optional[UnifiedTask]:
        pop_map = {
            "download": self.queue_adapter.pop_download,
            "process": self.queue_adapter.pop_process,
            "upload": self.queue_adapter.pop_upload,
        }
        pop_fn = pop_map.get(stage)
        if pop_fn is None:

from __future__ import annotations

import multiprocessing
import os
from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor
from concurrent.futures.process import BrokenProcessPool
from pathlib import Path
from threading import RLock
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional


def _reconfigure_stdio_utf8() -> None:
    for stream_name in ("stdout", "stderr"):
        stream = getattr(os.sys, stream_name, None)
        if stream is None:
            continue
        reconfigure = getattr(stream, "reconfigure", None)
        if callable(reconfigure):
            try:
                reconfigure(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
            except Exception:
                continue


def _apply_env(overrides: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> Dict[str, Optional[str]]:
    snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]] = {}
    for key, value in (overrides or {}).items():
        snapshot[key] = os.environ.get(key)
        if value:
            os.environ[key] = str(value)
        elif key in os.environ:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
    return snapshot


def _restore_env(snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]]) -> None:
    for key, value in snapshot.items():
        if value is None:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
        else:
            os.environ[key] = value


def _set_repo_root(repo_root: str) -> str:
    resolved = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
    if resolved not in os.sys.path:
        os.sys.path.insert(0, resolved)
    os.chdir(resolved)
    return resolved


def _child_initializer(repo_root: str, base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> None:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _apply_env(base_env)
    _set_repo_root(repo_root)


def _warmup_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        warmed = pipeline_module.warm_pipeline_runtime(output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]))
        return {"warmed": bool(warmed)}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


def _execute_pipeline_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        success = pipeline_module.run_pipeline_request(
            input_path=str(payload["input_path"]),
            output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]),
            model=payload.get("model"),
            file_encoding=payload.get("file_encoding"),
            enable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("enable_preprocess", False)),
            disable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("disable_preprocess", False)),
            clip_text=payload.get("clip_text"),
            clip_text_file=payload.get("clip_text_file"),
            forum_post_info_json=payload.get("forum_post_info_json"),
            organize_delete_original=payload.get("organize_delete_original"),
        )
        if not success:
            raise RuntimeError("warm internal pipeline returned False")
        return {"success": True}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


class InternalPipelineWarmRunner:
    def __init__(
        self,
        *,
        repo_root: str,
        output_dir: str,
        pool_size: int = 1,
        warmup_on_start: bool = True,
        base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None,
        logger: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.repo_root = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
        self.output_dir = str(Path(output_dir).resolve())
        self.pool_size = max(1, int(pool_size))
        self.warmup_on_start = bool(warmup_on_start)
        self.base_env = dict(base_env or {})
        self.logger = logger
        self._executor: Optional[ProcessPoolExecutor] = None
        self._lock = RLock()

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if self._executor is not None:
                return
            context = multiprocessing.get_context("spawn")
            self._executor = ProcessPoolExecutor(
                max_workers=self.pool_size,
                mp_context=context,
                initializer=_child_initializer,
                initargs=(self.repo_root, self.base_env),
            )
            if self.warmup_on_start:
                for _ in range(self.pool_size):
                    self._executor.submit(
                        _warmup_job,
                        {
                            "repo_root": self.repo_root,
                            "output_dir": self.output_dir,
                            "env": {},
                        },
                    )
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info(
                    "internal warm runner started: pool_size=%s warmup_on_start=%s",
                    self.pool_size,
                    self.warmup_on_start,
                )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            executor = self._executor
            self._executor = None
        if executor is not None:
            executor.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info("internal warm runner stopped")

    def execute(self, *, payload: Dict[str, Any], timeout_seconds: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if self._executor is None:
            self.start()
        executor = self._executor
        if executor is None:
            raise RuntimeError("warm runner executor unavailable")

        try:
            future = executor.submit(_execute_pipeline_job, payload)
            return future.result(timeout=timeout_seconds)
        except BrokenProcessPool as exc:
            self.stop()
            raise RuntimeError(f"warm runner process pool broke: {exc}") from exc

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import os


@dataclass
class VideoPipelineConfig:
    output_dir: str = "output"
    stop_on_error: bool = True
    keep_intermediate_files: bool = False

    @classmethod
    def from_env(cls, output_dir: str) -> "VideoPipelineConfig":
        stop_on_error = os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_STOP_ON_ERROR", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
        keep_intermediate = (
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_KEEP_INTERMEDIATE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
        )
        return cls(
            output_dir=output_dir,
            stop_on_error=stop_on_error,
            keep_intermediate_files=keep_intermediate,
        )

## 8. 方案B的执行顺序

### 阶段1：恢复可导入的内置流水线骨架

目标：让 `domain.video.pipeline` 能导入、测试能收集。

产出：

- `domain/video/stages/` 基础目录
- `StageResult` 与通用工具
- `__init__` 导出函数与模块

### 阶段2：按业务主链迁移 stage 实现

建议顺序：

1. `stage0_clean`
2. `stage1_transcode`
3. `stage2_silence`
4. `stage4_asr`
5. `stage5_ai_text`
6. `stage6_clip`
7. `stage6_5_resub`
8. `stage7_correct`
9. `stage7_subtitle`
10. `stage8_cover`
11. `stage9_organize`
12. `stage3_repair` 作为算法增强后置项补齐，但在骨架阶段必须先提供最小可运行实现

说明：`stage3` 当前并不是 OpenClaw 主链关键路径，优先级低于 2/4/5/6/7/8/9。

### 阶段3：统一资源生命周期与 ready 治理

目标：把重资源预加载、资源所有权、并发锁和 ready 状态做成 worker 内部能力。

实践方式：

- 在 worker 启动时初始化模型与工具实例
- 通过依赖注入或受控 registry 注入到 stage

from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path

import pytest

from apps.api.openclaw_client import run_openclaw_video_task, submit_openclaw_video_task, wait_for_openclaw_result


class _FakeResponse:
    def __init__(self, status_code: int, payload):
        self.status_code = status_code
        self._payload = payload
        self.text = str(payload)

    def json(self):
        return self._payload


class _FakeSession:
    def __init__(self, post_responses=None, get_responses=None) -> None:
        self.post_responses = list(post_responses or [])
        self.get_responses = list(get_responses or [])
        self.post_calls = []
        self.get_calls = []

    def post(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        self.post_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
        if not self.post_responses:
            raise AssertionError("unexpected post call")
        return self.post_responses.pop(0)

    def get(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        self.get_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
        if not self.get_responses:
            raise AssertionError("unexpected get call")
        return self.get_responses.pop(0)


def test_submit_openclaw_video_task_posts_expected_form(tmp_path) -> None:
    video = tmp_path / "sample.mp4"
    video.write_bytes(b"video")
    session = _FakeSession(
        post_responses=[
            _FakeResponse(
                201,
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": "task-123",
                    "openclaw_result_url": "/api/tasks/task-123/openclaw-result",
                },
            )
        ]
    )

    payload = submit_openclaw_video_task(
        api_base="http://127.0.0.1:18100",
        video_path=video,
        api_token="token-1",
        stage5_model_name="yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4",
        extra_form={"metadata": {"source": "test"}},
        session=session,
    )

    assert payload.get("task_id") == "task-123"
    call = session.post_calls[0]
    assert call["url"] == "http://127.0.0.1:18100/api/tasks/upload-video"
    assert call["headers"]["Authorization"] == "Bearer token-1"
    assert call["data"]["stage5_model_name"] == "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"
    assert call["data"]["metadata"] == '{"source": "test"}'
    uploaded_name, _, uploaded_content_type = call["files"]["file"]
    assert uploaded_name == "sample.mp4"
    assert uploaded_content_type == "video/mp4"


def test_wait_for_openclaw_result_polls_until_completed(monkeypatch) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    session = _FakeSession(
        get_responses=[
            _FakeResponse(
                200,
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": "task-123",

                    "task_id": "task-123",

                },
            ),
        ]
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.api.openclaw_client.time.sleep", lambda _seconds: None)

    payload = wait_for_openclaw_result(
        api_base="http://127.0.0.1:18100",
        task_id="task-123",
        poll_interval_seconds=0.2,
        session=session,
    )

    assert payload.get("openclaw_result", {}).get("status") == "completed"
    assert len(session.get_calls) == 2

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import mimetypes
from pathlib import Path
import time
from typing import Any, Mapping

import requests


def _normalize_api_base(api_base: str) -> str:
    text = str(api_base or "").strip().rstrip("/")
    if not text:
        raise ValueError("api_base is required")
    return text


def _resolve_api_url(api_base: str, path: str) -> str:
    base = _normalize_api_base(api_base)
    suffix = str(path or "").strip()
    if not suffix:
        return base
    if not suffix.startswith("/"):
        suffix = "/" + suffix
    return base + suffix


def _build_auth_headers(api_token: str) -> dict[str, str]:
    token = str(api_token or "").strip()
    if not token:
        return {}
    return {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}"}


def _response_json(response: Any) -> dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        payload = response.json()
    except Exception as exc:
        status_code = getattr(response, "status_code", "unknown")
        text = str(getattr(response, "text", "") or "").strip()
        raise RuntimeError(f"api returned non-json response: status={status_code} body={text}") from exc
    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
        raise RuntimeError(f"api returned invalid payload type: {type(payload)!r}")
    return payload


def _ensure_success_payload(payload: Mapping[str, Any], response: Any, context: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
    body = dict(payload or {})
    if bool(body.get("success")):
        return body
    status_code = getattr(response, "status_code", "unknown")
    error = str(body.get("error") or "").strip() or f"{context} failed"
    raise RuntimeError(f"{context} failed: status={status_code} error={error}")


def _coerce_form_value(value: Any) -> str:
    if isinstance(value, (dict, list)):
        return json.dumps(value, ensure_ascii=False)
    if value is None:
        return ""
    return str(value)


def submit_openclaw_video_task(
    api_base: str,
    video_path: str | Path,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    task_id: str = "",
    source: str = "openclaw_client",
    stage5_model_name: str = "",
    extra_form: Mapping[str, Any] | None = None,
    timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    client = session or requests
    file_path = Path(video_path).expanduser()
    if not file_path.exists() or not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"video file not found: {file_path}")

    form: dict[str, str] = {"source": source}
    if task_id:
        form["task_id"] = str(task_id).strip()
    if stage5_model_name:
        form["stage5_model_name"] = str(stage5_model_name).strip()
    for key, value in dict(extra_form or {}).items():
        text = _coerce_form_value(value)
        if text:
            form[str(key)] = text

    content_type = mimetypes.guess_type(file_path.name)[0] or "application/octet-stream"
    with file_path.open("rb") as file_handle:
        response = client.post(
            _resolve_api_url(api_base, "/api/tasks/upload-video"),
            data=form,
            files={"file": (file_path.name, file_handle, content_type)},
            headers=_build_auth_headers(api_token),
            timeout=max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds)),
        )
    payload = _response_json(response)
    return _ensure_success_payload(payload, response, context="submit openclaw video task")


def fetch_openclaw_result(
    api_base: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    client = session or requests
    resolved_task_id = str(task_id or "").strip()
    if not resolved_task_id:
        raise ValueError("task_id is required")

    response = client.get(
        _resolve_api_url(api_base, f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}/openclaw-result"),
        headers=_build_auth_headers(api_token),
        timeout=max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds)),
    )
    payload = _response_json(response)
    return _ensure_success_payload(payload, response, context="fetch openclaw result")


def wait_for_openclaw_result(
    api_base: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
    poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
    request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    deadline = time.time() + max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds))
    while True:
        payload = fetch_openclaw_result(
            api_base=api_base,
            task_id=task_id,
            api_token=api_token,
            timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
            session=session,
        )
        result = payload.get("openclaw_result") if isinstance(payload.get("openclaw_result"), dict) else {}
        status = str(result.get("status") or "").strip().lower()
        if status in {"completed", "failed", "cancelled"}:
            return payload
        if time.time() >= deadline:
            raise TimeoutError(f"wait openclaw result timed out: task_id={task_id} status={status or 'unknown'}")
        time.sleep(max(0.2, float(poll_interval_seconds)))


def run_openclaw_video_task(
    api_base: str,
    video_path: str | Path,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    task_id: str = "",
    source: str = "openclaw_client",
    stage5_model_name: str = "",
    extra_form: Mapping[str, Any] | None = None,
    wait: bool = True,
    submit_timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,
    wait_timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
    poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
    request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    submitted = submit_openclaw_video_task(
        api_base=api_base,
        video_path=video_path,
        api_token=api_token,
        task_id=task_id,
        source=source,
        stage5_model_name=stage5_model_name,
        extra_form=extra_form,
        timeout_seconds=submit_timeout_seconds,
        session=session,
    )
    output = {"submit": submitted}
    if not wait:
        return output

    resolved_task_id = str(submitted.get("task_id") or "").strip()
    if not resolved_task_id:
        raise RuntimeError("submit response missing task_id")
    output["result"] = wait_for_openclaw_result(
        api_base=api_base,
        task_id=resolved_task_id,
        api_token=api_token,
        timeout_seconds=wait_timeout_seconds,
        poll_interval_seconds=poll_interval_seconds,
        request_timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
        session=session,
    )
    return output

    "run_openclaw_video_task",

## 7. 方案B的核心改造点

### 6.1 重建 `domain/video/stages/`

这是第一阻塞项，也是方案B起点。

必须补齐至少以下文件：

- `domain/video/stages/__init__.py`
- `domain/video/stages/base.py`
- `domain/video/stages/utils.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage0_clean.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage1_transcode.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage2_silence.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage3_repair.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage4_asr.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage5_ai_text.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage6_clip.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage6_5_resub.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage7_correct.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage7_subtitle.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage8_cover.py`
- `domain/video/stages/stage9_organize.py`

### 6.2 将旧 `pre/stage/*` 逻辑迁移为新 stage 实现

迁移不是简单复制，而是做三件事：

1. 去除交互式输入
2. 去除脚本式全局副作用
3. 收敛为可测试、可编排、可观测的单阶段函数

### 6.3 让 `VideoPipeline` 真正可运行

需要让 `domain/video/pipeline.py` 成为稳定编排器，具备：

- 顺序执行
- 阶段上下文透传
- performance tracker 与 resource monitor 挂接
- stage 失败时的可诊断信息
- artifacts / manifest 汇总
- 对当前测试已锁定的 `method` / `engine` / `fallback_used` / `strict_rejected` 等字段保持契约清晰

### 6.4 让 worker 切到内置 pipeline

最终目标是：

- 通用视频任务主路径不再调用 `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py`
- 通用视频任务主路径不再依赖 `InternalPipelineWarmRunner` 作为主执行器
- 通用视频任务直接以 `VideoPipeline` 执行
- `ExternalVideoCommandAdapter` 不再进入通用视频主链；是否仓库级彻底移除，作为单独清理决策执行

### 6.5 收敛结果协议

OpenClaw 只应该拿到稳定的结构化结果，而不是猜测内部文件名。

最终对外稳定协议建议至少包含：

- 主成片
- 字幕文件
- 封面图/封面视频相关产物
- `clip_text`
- `script`
- `render_manifest`
- 处理日志
- 失败信息与最后完成 stage

并且要补上正式契约：

- `schema_version`
- 必填字段清单
- artifacts 命名规则
- OpenClaw 读取结果的契约测试

### 7.6 建立平台无关入口

除了 worker 内主链切换，还需要把“外部怎么调用 CloneCut”做成稳定接口。

建议至少落两类入口：

- `HTTP API`：给 OpenClaw、MCP server、远程 agent 调用
- `CLI`：给 shell skill、本地 wrapper、调试与运维调用

这一步的目标不是替代 API，而是把“平台调用协议”从 OpenClaw 专属约定，提升为 CloneCut 通用能力。

### 7.7 生成 Skill 但不把 Skill 当内核

方案B允许并鼓励提供 skill，但 skill 的位置必须摆正：

- skill 是调用封装
token_count #303 04:08:51
total_tokens=2273156
total 2273156in 2268291out 29484reason 6045
